              if (!this.selectedCategories.includes(category)) {\n                        this.selectedCategories.push(category);\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    this.selectedCategories = this.selectedCategories.filter(c => c !== category);\n                }\n            }\n\n            generatePersonalizedPlaylist() {\n                this.intention = this.selectedCategories.forEach(category => {\n                    const content = this.contentDatabase[category] || [];\n                    const filtered = content.filter(item => \n                        item.mood.includes(this.selectedMood)\n                    );\n                    playlist.push(...filtered);\n                });\n\n                // Add amplification-based content\n        return playlist\n                    .sort((a, b) => b.vibration - a.vibration)\n                    .slice(0, 10);\n            }\n\n            getFrequencyBasedContent(amplifications) {\n                const frequencyContent = [];\n                \n                if (amplifications.amplifications.frequencies.length > 0) {\n                    const targetFreq = amplifications.amplifications.frequencies[0].baseFrequency;\n                    \n                    Object.values(this.contentDatabase).flat().forEach(content => {\n                        if (Math.abs(content.frequency - targetFreq) < 50) {\n                            frequencyContent.push(content);\n                        }\n                    });\n                }\n\n                return frequencyContent.slice(0, 3);\n            }\n\n            showAmplificationAnalysis() {\n                document.getElementById(\'amplificationPanel\').style.display = \'block\';\n                \n                // Simulate amplification analysis based on intention and mood\n                const baseValues = {\n                    peaceful: { consciousness: 75, heart: 90, frequency: animation\n                this.animateValue(\'consciousnessLevel\', 0, values.consciousness, 1500);\n                this.animateValue(\'heartCoherence\', 0, values.heart, 1500);\n                this.animateValue(\'frequencyMatch\', 0, values.frequency, 1500);\n                this.animateValue(\'crystalSync\', 0, values.crystal, 1500);\n                \n                // Update vibration : avgVibration > 40 ? \'Moderate\' : \'Low\';\n                document.getElementById(\'vibrationText\').textContent = vibrationLevel;\n            }\n\n            animateValue(elementId, start, end, duration) {\n                const element = document.getElementById(elementId);\n                const range = end - start;\n                const increment = range / (duration / 16);\n                let current = start;\n                \n                const timer = setInterval(() => {\n                    current += increment;\n                    if ((increment > 0 && current >= end) || (increment < 0 && current <= end)) {\n                        current = end;\n                        clearInterval(timer);\n                    }\n                    element.textContent = `${Math.round(current)}%`;\n                }, 16);\n            }\n\n            displayPlaylist() {\n                document.getElementById(\'playlistPanel\').style.display = \'block\';\n                \n                const container = document.getElementById(\'playlistItems\');\n                container.innerHTML = \'\';\n                \n                this.currentPlaylist.forEach((item,
